# Frontend Test Coverage Catalog

Maps implemented tests under `frontend/test/` to product areas aligned with `frontend/lib/core` and `frontend/lib/features/*`.

## How to read this document

- **Test layer**: `UI (widget)` exercises screens/widgets; `Logic (unit)` covers domain/data/presentation logic without full UI; `Integration` spans multiple layers; `Boundary` hits live Supabase.
- **Pass**: conditions that must hold for the test to succeed.
- **Fail**: what a broken implementation looks like from the test's perspective.
- Use blank rows in your mental checklist: any user story or RPC path with **no matching scenario** here is currently untested on the frontend.

## Summary

| Feature                               | Logic (unit) | UI (widget) | Integration | Boundary |    Total |
| ------------------------------------- | -----------: | ----------: | ----------: | -------: | -------: |
| Core                                  |           29 |           2 |           0 |       11 |   **42** |
| Auth                                  |          105 |          64 |          32 |       45 |  **246** |
| Settings (Org & Branch Management UI) |           97 |          85 |          48 |       36 |  **266** |
| Patients                              |          311 |          50 |          19 |       48 |  **428** |
| Appointments                          |          150 |          71 |          28 |       10 |  **259** |
| Visits                                |          150 |          85 |          25 |        0 |  **260** |
| Startup                               |           15 |           2 |          10 |        0 |   **27** |
| Shared / Foundations Demo             |            0 |           8 |           0 |        0 |    **8** |
| **All**                               |              |             |             |          | **1543** |

### Untested scenarios (inferred from catalog gaps)

_Inferred only from patterns and omissions in this document — not from a full repo scan._

- UI (widget): reusable widgets beyond searchable dropdown (button, dialog, data table, form field, modifiable fields, unsaved-changes guard, snackbar) — not in this category (partial overlap with Shared demo tests)
- Logic (unit): paginated list notifier / table pagination — no scenarios
- Logic (unit): user-facing error mapping utilities — no scenarios
- Logic (unit): Supabase initializer lifecycle (beyond probe URLs / debug bootstrap flags) — no scenarios
- Boundary: PostgREST read contract for `patients` table (catalog lists staff/org/branch/roles only) — no scenarios
- Integration: core cross-cutting infrastructure — no scenarios in this category

### Untested scenarios (inferred from catalog gaps)

_Inferred only from patterns and omissions in this document — not from a full repo scan._

- UI / Integration: appointment placeholder page — no scenarios
- Walk-in appointment type — no scenarios (catalog is planned-type oriented)
- Booking outside branch working hours — no Logic/UI scenario keywords
- Boundary: 10 live Supabase scenarios vs 36+ Settings / 48+ Patients — thinner appointment repository boundary coverage
- Concurrent booking / double-submit — no Integration or Boundary scenarios
- Calendar page exists in catalog but month/week navigation edge cases are not distinguished

### Untested scenarios (inferred from catalog gaps)

_Inferred only from patterns and omissions in this document — not from a full repo scan._

- Boundary (live Supabase): visit RPC contract suite — no scenarios in this category
- Integration: full multi-role visit journey with live backend — acceptance tests use mocks
- UI (widget): visit documentation page shell loading states — partial coverage via SOAP/treatment widgets
- Logic (unit): specialty form schema provider — covered indirectly via repository/widget tests
